0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They say <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">it's better to</strong></em><span style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"> give</span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> than to </strong></em></span>receive. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">人们说施<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比</strong>受<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">有福</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p </strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>way</strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> better to</strong></em></span> do it badly <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">than </strong></em></span>not <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: to</strong></em></span> do it right than <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">to </strong></em></span>do it fast.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">正确地做<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">比</strong>快速地做<strong style="box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;">一生也许只会遇到一次</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">nce-in-a-lifetime adj. 一生中难得一次的；千载难逢的；难能可贵的</strong></p><p style="white-space: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">而这批T恤是我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">百年难得一遇的</strong>机会。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">co·a lesce </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌkəʊəˈles  / VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 联合；合并；结合</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使…联合；使…合并</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The puddles had coalesced into a small stream. 地面上水洼子里的水汇流成了一条小溪。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That material rapidly coalesces, and bingo, you've got a moon.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些物质迅速结合，没错，之后就形成了月球。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">deb·ris </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈdebriː  ; ˈdeɪbriː  ; NAmE dəˈbriː  / NOUN [uncountable ]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 散落的碎片, 残骸</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Clear away leaves and other garden debris from the pond. 把池塘里的树叶和其他庭园垃圾清除干净。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Debris from the explosion broke a window.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">爆炸产生的碎片击中了一扇窗户。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">isol·ate </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈaɪsəleɪt / VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使孤立；使绝缘；使隔离</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 隔离种群</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 孤立；隔离</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 隔离的；孤立的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Patients with the disease should be isolated. 这种病的患者应予以隔离。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">dis·perse </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ dɪˈspɜːs  ; NAmE dɪˈspɜːrs  / VERB</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. &amp; vi. (使)散开, 驱散</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The crowd dispersed when the rain fell suddenly.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当天空突然下雨时，群众就四散而去。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They（elephants） disperse seeds in their copious droppings.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大象在粪便中散播种子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">skip </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/skɪp/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 跳, 蹦;跳绳</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 略过; 跳过; 漏过</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 跳, 蹦</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is skipping the individual sprint event.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他将不会参加个人短跑项目。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We tend to skip right over those.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们更愿意跳过这些东西。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Homo sa·pi·ens </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌhəʊməʊ ˈsæpienz /  ( technical 术语 ) the kind or speciesof human that exists now 智人（全部现代人的属和种）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 智人(现代人的学名)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">meager</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'mi:gə/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 贫乏的；瘦的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 兆</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Eh, meager touches, but I get by.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时运不济 但我熬过来了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The diet should be suitable, being neither too rich nor too meager.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">饮食应该适当， 既不能太油腻也不能太粗淡。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" 0.5em;border-top-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-right-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);border-bottom-color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="vertical-align: middle;padding: 8px 0px 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Monday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;line-height: 2;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">As fa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r a</span></span>s we know, aroun<span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span> 4,500 million year<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: 196);box-sizing: border-box;">ck</span></span> tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> we li<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ve o</span></span>n coalesced from</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> the dus<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>n<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> debris lef<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>ver from the formatio<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n of o</span></span>ur sun. Withou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> airplanes, pizza delivery, </span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">or the Internet, things moved more slowly across th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e ear</span></span>ly earth than they do today.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Fo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r e</span></span>xample, from isolated puddle<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s o</span></span>f water, the oceans formed over the course of 400 to </span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">800 million years.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">据我们所知，大约在</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">45</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">亿年前，我们赖以生存的这块岩石是由太阳形成时留下的灰尘和碎片凝聚而成的。那个时候没有飞机，没有外卖，也没有互联网。早期，地球上的事物移动的速度比今天慢。比如，要从一个孤立的小水坑变成海洋，要经历</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">亿到</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">8</span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">亿年的时间。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">That’s how long i<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span>woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> take for your hair to gr<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ow a</span></span>round th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e ear</span></span>th– twice.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是你的头发在地球周围生长所需时间的两倍。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">In tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> same time, bacterial life did sprea<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>cross the watery globe.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">与此同时细菌生命在全球的水体中传播开来。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Higher</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> plan<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ts a</span></span>n<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>nimal<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s, o</span></span>n th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e o</span></span>ther hand, took much longer to develo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">p a</span></span>n<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> disperse.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">另一方面高等植物和动物花费了更长时间进化和传播。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">But we’re</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> going to skip those 3 billion years (during which your hair woul<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d ha</span></span>ve grown to the moon)</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> tal<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span>bou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> us, Homo sapiens. We were much faster tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>ur own hair, which woul<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> <span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">h</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">a</span></span>ve</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> grown a meager 27km in the 180,000 years we too<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">k</span></span> to cross Africa an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(68, 114, 196);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> reach all the unfrozen</span>﻿<span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> continents.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">但是我们将跳过那</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> 30 </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">亿年（在此期间你的头发会长到月球上）并谈论我们自己，智人。我们的头发比我们自己的头发快得多，在我们穿越非洲到达所有未冻结大陆的</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> 180,000 </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年里，头发会长出微薄的</span><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> 27 </span><span style="font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">公里。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was very dark and dusty and draughty and they stepped from rafter to rafter without a word except when they whispered to one another, "We're opposite your attic now" or "this must be halfway through our house". And neither of them stumbled and the candles didn't go out, and at last they came where they could see a little door in the brick wall on their right. There was no bolt or handle on this side of it, of course, for the door had been made for getting in, not for getting out; but there was a catch (as there often is on the inside of a cupboard door) which they felt sure they would be able to turn.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">黑暗而通风的隧道里积着厚厚的灰尘。他们踩着椽子悄然而行，偶尔互相耳语一句“到你家阁楼对面了”，或者“走到我家房子的中间了”。两人都没有跌倒过，蜡烛也没有熄灭过，最后，他们停住了，看见右面的砖墙上有扇小门。门的这一面既无门闩也无把手，显然，那门是做来让人进屋，而不是让人走出去的。但门上有个挂钩（像衣柜门上常见的那种），他们觉得完全能够打开。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你好，史蒂文。安妮说，你和茱莉亚吵架了，有这回事吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那是真的。昨天我们吵了一架，那天她责备我没有准备晚饭，但那天是轮到她做饭呢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 这就是你们吵架的原因吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 没错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你们两个总为一些小事争吵。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那件事不是我的错，可她竟然对我说“你真丢人”。我肺都要气炸了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你现在还在生她的气吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 老实说，我不生气了。而且还有点后悔我做的事。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你会向她道歉吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 没门，应该道歉的是她。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Hello, Steven. Annie said that you and Julia have had a quarrel, haven't you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That's true. We had an argument yesterday. She blamed me for not preparing the supper that day, but it was her turn to cook the dinner.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: That's the reason why you fought?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Yes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: You two are always quarrelling over little things.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: That wasn't my fault, but she said "you are a disgrace" to me. I'm about to explode.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Are you still mad at her now?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: To be honest, I'm not and I regret a little for what I've done</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Will you apologize to her?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No way. It's her who should apologize.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This is to be ____________ , so I'll pay for everything. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">该我请客了，一切由我来付钱。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">my treat</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="text-align: center;"><br/></section>style="text-align: center;"><br/></section><section style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《古墓奇兵》</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">*tight 反义词为 loose</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">同义表达：a tight hold/grip</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His mother kept a <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">tight </strong></em></span><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>hold</strong></em></span> on his hand.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他母亲<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">紧紧</strong>抓住他的手。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：If you <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>hold</strong></em></span> it too <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">tightly</strong></em></span>, you crush it. If you hold it too loosely, it flies away.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果握<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太紧</strong>，会捏死它；握太松，它就飞了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：<span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong>Hold</strong></em></span> it a little bit <span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><em><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">tightly</strong></em></span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">握得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">紧</strong>一点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Ah, ignore that, things <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fall apart</strong></em></span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈæɡrɪˌkʌltʃə $ -ər/  n.[农] 农业；农艺，[农学] 农学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Agriculture is a mainstay of the economy.农业是经济的支柱</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. scatter /ˈskætə $ -ər/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi.分散，散开；[军] 散射spread around . spread about</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt.[军] 使散射；使散开，使分散；使散播，使撒播disject . disperse</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.分散；散播，撒播dissemination . decentralization</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He is scattering his money about. 他在挥霍钱财。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Scatter clothes about the house .把衣服乱丢在家中。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">scatter across 分散（在各地）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. tasty</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈteɪsti/ adj.好吃的；〈口〉有风味的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4. regional </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈriːdʒənəl/ adj.地区的；局部的；整个地区的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">regional literature 地方文学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. migration </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/maɪˈɡreɪʃən/ n.[动] [地质] 迁移；移民；移动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Why is there a migration of industry from urban areas towards relatively rural ones?为什么工业从城市地区向相对农村地区转移？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. domesticated  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/dəˈmestɪˈkeɪtɪd/ adj.家养的；驯服的；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When was the cat first domesticated? 猫最开始是什么时候被驯养的？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7. BC公元前(before Christ)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">AD公元（源自拉丁语 Anno Domini） 2021 AD</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8. speculate /ˈspekjəleɪt/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi.推测；投机；思索guess . venture</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt.推断understand . conclude</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Speculate about 思考</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">People have been speculating about interstellar flight for years.多年来，人们一直在思索星际飞行。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">9. Fertile Crescent</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈfɜːtaɪl //ˈkresənt/新月沃地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">指伊拉克两河流域连接叙利亚一带地中海东岸的一片弧形地区,为上古文明发源地之一</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">10. roughly </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈrʌfli/ adv.粗糙地；概略地 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Martin makes roughly $150,000 a year.马丁的年收入约为15万美元。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">11. blistering </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈblɪstərɪŋ/adj.猛烈的；极热的，极快的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blistering summer days炎热的夏日</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">12. The Bubonic plague </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bjuːˌbɒnɪk ˈpleɪɡ/ 鼠疫；黑死病</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">是人类历史上最严重的瘟疫之一。起源于亚洲西南部，约在1340年代散布到欧洲，而“黑死病”之名是当时欧洲的称呼。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">13. printing press 印刷机；印刷术</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">14. populace </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈpɒpjələs $ ˈpɑː-/n.平民百姓；民众</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A large group of the American populace attends church regularly.一大批美国民众定期去教堂做礼拜。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">15. mania </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈmeɪniə/ n.狂热；躁狂症</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A mania for a game called Nibs ran through the school.一款名为Nibs的游戏在全校掀起了一股狂热。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">16. Hula hoop</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> /'hu:lə hu:p/ n.呼啦圈</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: i</span></span>t from the Fertile Crescen<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> to both the Atlantic and <span style="color: rgb(255, 192, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">the </span>Pacific by roughly 2500BC.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/> </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在许多这样的地方，我们能够发展出农业等有用的做法，但因为我们分散在全球各地，最好的想法和最美味的地区性食物只能通过贸易或人类迁徙才能获得市场。例如，大约在公元前</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">8500</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年左右，小麦被利用做成粥。事实上，一些人猜测它可能是用来酿造啤酒的，但无论是哪种方式，小麦都是在公元前</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">2500</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">年左右从新月沃土地带到达大西洋和太平洋的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: the Middle Ages!</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: 240);box-sizing: border-box;">pe</span></span> in less tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n a</span></span> hundred years, bringing death and literacy to the populace before their hair could have even grown 15 meters. In the 20th century, mania for both the Beatles and the Hula hoop race<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span>round the world in a year or two.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/> </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">在不到一百年的时间里，鼠疫和印刷机分别在欧洲蔓延开来，在他们的头发还没有长到</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">15</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">米之前就给他们带来了死亡和文字。在</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">20</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">世纪，对披头士和呼啦圈的狂热在一两年内风靡全球。</span></p><p style="line-height: 19px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">"I'm game if you are," said Polly, just as she had said before. Both felt that it was becoming very serious, but neither would draw back. Digory pushed round the catch with some difficultly. The door swung open and the sudden daylight made them blink. Then, with a great shock, they saw that they were looking, not into a deserted attic, but into a furnished room. But it seemed empty enough. It was dead silent. Polly's curiosity got the better of her. She blew out her candle and stepped out into the strange room, making no more noise than a mouse.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">“只要你愿意，我就愿意。”波莉又搬出她的口头禅。两人都知道，他们正处在紧要关头，但谁也没有后退。迪格雷费了一番劲才把挂钩打开。门一开，突然射来的自然光使他们忍不住眨了眨眼。接着，他们非常惊奇地发现，面前不是一间废弃的阁楼，而是一个陈设完整的房间。但似乎又是空荡荡的，一派死寂。波莉在好奇心的驱使下吹灭了蜡烛，像耗子一样悄悄地走进了那间奇怪的屋子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你最近有没有看什么好电影？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我已经好久没去看电影了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 怎么？你当学生时可是个地道的电影狂。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 而现在我愿意呆在家里看电视。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Have you seen any good movies lately? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It's ages since I went to see a film. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Why? You were a real movie buff when you were a student. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: But now I would stay at home watching TV. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's __________ we were apart at school. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">从学校分开后已经很久没见了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ages since</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;font-size: 18px;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>7.27 每日一句：Nothing can be done. 无计可施。</strong></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: center;margin-top: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">There is no formula for success, except perhaps an unconditional acceptance of life and what it brings.</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;transform: style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: rgb(255, 255, 255);">ə</span>/，不可卷舌；</strong></span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. perhap</strong><span style="font-size: 14px;text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">s an u</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. <strong style="font-size: 14px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：</strong>There is no (magic) formula for XX/doing XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做...没有公式/规律</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：There is no XX for noun./doing XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</strong></span>：Just as <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">there is no magic formula for</strong></em></span> writing a great short story...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">正如写一篇伟大的短篇小说<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有什么神奇的公式</strong>...</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句</span></strong>：<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">There's </strong></em></span>also <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">no magic formula for</strong></em></span> living a life of purpose and of exploration. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">过一种有目的、有探索的生活，也<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有什么神奇的公式</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">There's </strong></em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">no magic formula for</strong></em></span> a perfect marriage.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">没有一个</strong>达到完美婚姻<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的神奇方法</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">There is no magic formula for </strong></em></span>passing exams—only hard work.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">根本没有</strong>通过考试<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的魔法</strong>—只有勤奋学习。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. formula noun. </strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">① 公式；方程式</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">formula </strong></em></span>for calculating distance</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">计算距离的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">公式</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">The bigger <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">formula </strong></em></span>should embrace or enclose a smaller <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">formula</strong></em></span>.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">大<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">公式</strong>应该和小<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">公式</strong>是兼容的。</span></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: 400;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.6231481" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcu6qf1KGYS32YDHnapY5mmlHZG2f2k7UqjiawmgZicA5AS7w6EGvYU3K4nYbveF3d8Hl7erf0FX4tw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="font-weight: 400;text-align: right;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">图片源自《耶鲁大学开放课程》</span></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="font-weight: 400;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">语音课有同学对美音中的/ɔ/和/ɑ/不太理解。其实很多美国人并不区分这两个音，一律发成后者。我也一直习惯这么发。但它们也有区别。这么说吧，dog的音标是/dɔg/，很多美国人会发成/dɑg/。但反过来，father的音标/'fɑðər/就不能发成/fɔðər/。说到底还是那句话：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一个符号对应一个音，记住符号发音然后以字典为准就没毛病了。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">可以看看下面这篇文章：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653513492&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=0fefe4bc2fc22c455549b0c19792884e&amp;chksm=f7e8a7d9c09f2ecf8ad1fbb9134dc7978844b311697ecd906c3752fcc5031cad94adaeee9f64&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="一篇文章告诉你DJ音标和KK音标的不同"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一篇文章告诉你DJ音标和KK音标的不同</strong></a><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">另外，朗文在线词典中的/ɒː/其实就是/ɔ/。另另外，/ɑ/和/ɑː/是一回事。另另另外，不要把英音中包含/ɒ/和/ɔː/的词与美音中含/ɔ/和/ɑ/的词去一一对应。对应不上，也没有意义。再重复一遍：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一个符号一个音，记住符号发音后查字典（学音标的意义就是这么简单）。单词发音以权威词典的标音为准，配合全球发音去听。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5623188" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcu6qf1KGYS32YDHnapY5mmgouWusyjFbs9ljcolIT6Hj0TVhYjLVYfQhSXJaiatR5nf9hhiayJcJsA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="690" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：生活</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我如何做时间管理</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">有同学问我如何时间管理？怎么做到工作很忙、要照顾家庭，却仍能有时间读书看剧的？</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">其实这些“闲”事根本不花时间的。比如我看书一般是会利用坐地铁时、等孩子培训班下课时、睡觉前；跑步运动时看剧或听英语播客，做家务时也一定会外放播客或vlog。这些碎片时间看起来不起眼，积少成多，一周一月一年算下来也很可观。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">但实际上多数人都没有做时间的主人，却在一边抱怨自己“没时间”。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">比如，据我观察，几乎很少看到地铁里有看书的人，几乎都在刷手机。实际上这个时间用来看书真是极好的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">受方言影响，说英语总带“儿”化音怎么办？</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">其实想克服也并不难，就一条标准：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看单词拼写。</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">单词里只要没有字母r，无论英美，都不卷舌。</strong>所以像was、the、idea、famous、previous、precious等，不该卷的地方就不要卷。尤其要注意区分/ə/和/r/，前者舌身平整。</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">例外微乎其微，至今只发现一个单词：colonel。虽然拼写里没有字母r，但其美音是包含/r/的。其他基本没有例外。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p
