1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(192, 200, 209);padding: 10px;background-color: rgb(250, 250, 239);box-shadow: rgb(170, 170, 170) 0px 0px 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">很早以前我就发觉很多同学遇到一些问题无处求解。后来，我从2016年起在微博设立“Gwen为你答”板块，免费为大家答疑。几年来，遇到了不少共性的好问题。最近忽然想到，不如把微博上的答疑“搬”来公号，做个集合，供有同样疑问的宝子们查阅参考。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">想法不如行动，说干就干。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">我将近一年的答疑按照不同类别分成了<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">生活、学习</strong>（语音 口语 听力 原版书 写作）<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">和推荐</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">类</strong>。暂定每周三更新。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">答疑一直在继续。如果你有什么问题，可随时来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">微博TeacherGwen</strong>私信我。只要我能帮得上忙，都会尽力解答。</span></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">美音中的/ɔ/和/ɑ/</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">语音课有同学对美音中的/ɔ/和/ɑ/不太理解。其实很多美国人并不区分这两个音，一律发成后者。我也一直习惯这么发。但它们也有区别。这么说吧，dog的音标是/dɔg/，很多美国人会发成/dɑg/。但反过来，father的音标/'fɑðər/就不能发成/fɔðər/。说到底还是那句话：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一个符号对应一个音，记住符号发音然后以字典为准就没毛病了。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">可以看看下面这篇文章：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653513492&amp;idx=2&amp;sn=0fefe4bc2fc22c455549b0c19792884e&amp;chksm=f7e8a7d9c09f2ecf8ad1fbb9134dc7978844b311697ecd906c3752fcc5031cad94adaeee9f64&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="一篇文章告诉你DJ音标和KK音标的不同"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一篇文章告诉你DJ音标和KK音标的不同</strong></a><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">另外，朗文在线词典中的/ɒː/其实就是/ɔ/。另另外，/ɑ/和/ɑː/是一回事。另另另外，不要把英音中包含/ɒ/和/ɔː/的词与美音中含/ɔ/和/ɑ/的词去一一对应。对应不上，也没有意义。再重复一遍：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一个符号一个音，记住符号发音后查字典（学音标的意义就是这么简单）。单词发音以权威词典的标音为准，配合全球发音去听。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.5623188" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcu6qf1KGYS32YDHnapY5mmgouWusyjFbs9ljcolIT6Hj0TVhYjLVYfQhSXJaiatR5nf9hhiayJcJsA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="690" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.2449275" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKcu6qf1KGYS32YDHnapY5mmuHCPmFUCL8ibBRH25RibnrYibum5RA9bEwWicKC5SPlciaM2icfepaZ2lyOQ/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="690" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：生活</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我如何做时间管理</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">有同学问我如何时间管理？怎么做到工作很忙、要照顾家庭，却仍能有时间读书看剧的？</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">其实这些“闲”事根本不花时间的。比如我看书一般是会利用坐地铁时、等孩子培训班下课时、睡觉前；跑步运动时看剧或听英语播客，做家务时也一定会外放播客或vlog。这些碎片时间看起来不起眼，积少成多，一周一月一年算下来也很可观。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">但实际上多数人都没有做时间的主人，却在一边抱怨自己“没时间”。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">比如，据我观察，几乎很少看到地铁里有看书的人，几乎都在刷手机。实际上这个时间用来看书真是极好的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="align-items: center;display: flex;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;border-width: 0px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);overflow: hidden;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-webkit-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-moz-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);-o-transform: matrix(1, 0, -0.2, 1, 0, 0);border-style: solid;border-width: 0px;border-color: rgb(76, 68, 71);padding: 3px 5px 3px 20px;background-color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">答疑：学习</strong></p></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: auto;flex: 100 100 0%;border-width: 0px;height: auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;align-self: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 3px;margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;letter-spacing: 0px;color: rgb(76, 68, 71);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">受方言影响，说英语总带“儿”化音怎么办？</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">其实想克服也并不难，就一条标准：<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">看单词拼写。</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">单词里只要没有字母r，无论英美，都不卷舌。</strong>所以像was、the、idea、famous、previous、precious等，不该卷的地方就不要卷。尤其要注意区分/ə/和/r/，前者舌身平整。</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">例外微乎其微，至今只发现一个单词：colonel。虽然拼写里没有字母r，但其美音是包含/r/的。其他基本没有例外。</p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">往期内容：</p><p style='max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino a<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> nanomete</strong>r, <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">or</em> two <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">atoms</strong>,</span> <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">现在甚至一年都是很长的一段时间，每天有上百万的人乘坐飞机，</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: black;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">比如</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: black;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">In short</span></strong><span style="color: black;background: white;box-sizing: sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/> </span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"><br Why do we think the earth <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">is</em> 4,500,000,000 year</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">s old</span></span><span style="color: black;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">? Arial, sans-serif;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It was shaped, of course, like an attic, but furnished as a sitting-room. Every bit of the walls was lined with shelves and every bit of the shelves was full of books. A fire was burning in the grate (you remember that it was a very cold wet summer that year) and in front of the fire-place with its back towards them was a high-backed armchair. Between the chair and Polly, and filling most of the middle of the room, was a big table piled with all sorts of things printed books, and books of the sort you write in, and ink bottles and pens and sealing-wax and a microscope. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">屋子的形状很像阁楼，但又装饰得像起居室。沿墙摆满了架子，架上放满了书籍。壁炉里燃着火，（你还记得那年夏天又冷又湿吧？）火炉前面，一把高背扶手椅背对他们两人放着。在波莉和椅子之间，占据大部分空间的是一张堆着各种物什的大桌子——书、笔记薄、墨水瓶、钢笔、封蜡和一台显微镜。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 要不要一起去自然历史博物馆？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 你以前去过吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 去过好几次。那些种类繁多的展品让我印象深刻。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 走吧，好像蛮有趣的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Would you like to go to the natural history museum with me?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Have you ever been to it before?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes, lots of times. I was quite impressed by the wide variety of exhibitions they have.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Let's go. It sounds interesting.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I was quite ________ by the cleanliness of the hospital.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我对那所医院的清洁印象很深。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p </strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">di</strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">rection中的di-前缀可以有多种发音：</strong></p></section><section to move more quickly.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">随着空气上升，它可以<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">改变方向</strong>，开始移动得更快。</p><p border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1.inconsequential </strong>形容词</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">表示不重要的；微不足道的；不合理的；不合逻辑的； </p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">Seemingly <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">inconsequential</span> details can sometimes contain significant clues.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">貌似<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">无足轻重的</span>细节有时可能隐含着重大的线索。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The choice, in short, is between the </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">incomprehensible and the </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">inconsequential.</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">总之，就是介于令人费解和<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">毫无逻辑</span>之间。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;padding-right: 20px;padding-left: 20px;color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;padding-right: 20px;padding-left: 20px;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Everybody doesn't like him because he is an i<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">nfamous</span> liar.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">终于见到<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">声名狼藉的</span>" 八卦天后" 本尊了。</p></section></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;">4.exclusive </strong>形容词<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">①专有的，专用的；独有的，独占的；不愿接受（较低社会阶层的）新成员的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Times has been granted an <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">英释：of a high quality and expensive and therefore not often bought or used by most people</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, border-box;">it.</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他<span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">9.It's idiotic to get my hopes up.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我真是痴心妄想。</p><p border-box;">idiotic十分愚蠢的；白痴般的；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm sure I've seen way more <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">idiotic</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我确定我见过更<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">蠢的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get one's hopes up抱有期望；满怀希望；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> get your hopes up</span>. It probably won't happen.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">抱太大期望</span>，应该没那么好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They've <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">got Mr Mason's hopes up</span>, let him think he had a future.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">给了梅森先生希望</span>，让他以为又有了光明的未来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">10.Forget I mentioned it.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我没说吧；当我没提过；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-Nothing. <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">Forget I mentioned it. </span>It is not my place. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-What?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">- They had an affair.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-没事。<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">当我没提过。</span>这与我无关。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-他们之间有私情。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 30px 0% border-box;max-width: 100%;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1.inconsequential </strong>形容词</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">表示不重要的；微不足道的；不合理的；不合逻辑的； </p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;">Seemingly <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">inconsequential</span> details can sometimes contain significant clues.<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">貌似<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">无足轻重的</span>细节有时可能隐含着重大的线索。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The choice, in short, is between the </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">incomprehensible and the </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">inconsequential.</span></p><p style="white-space: style="box-sizing: border-box;">4.exclusive </strong>形容词<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">①专有的，专用的；独有的，独占的；不愿接受（较低社会阶层的）新成员的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">英释：limited to one person or group of people</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Times has been granted an <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">exclusive</span> interview.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">时报获得<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">独家</span>采访权。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He donated a lot of money to join the <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">exclusive</span> club.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他捐了很多钱以加入这个<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">入会严格的</span>俱乐部。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">②豪华的；昂贵的；高档的</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, 80);box-sizing: border-box;">英释：of a high quality and expensive and therefore not often bought or used by most people</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(80, 80, border-box;">7.do wonders</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">创造奇迹；取得惊人的成就</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Botox would <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">do wonders</span> for all those frown lines.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">肉毒素对那些皱纹<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">有显著效果</span>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know people say therapy's a waste of time, but you <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">did wonders </span>with my trust issues.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道人们都说心理治疗只不过是浪费时间，但是你在我的信任问题上<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">创造了奇迹</span>。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: inline;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="margin: 30px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;">9.It's idiotic to get my hopes up.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我真是痴心妄想。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">idiotic十分愚蠢的；白痴般的；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm sure I've seen way more <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">idiotic</span>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我确定我见过更<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">蠢的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get one's hopes up抱有期望；满怀希望；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Don't<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"> get your hopes up</span>. It probably won't happen.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">抱太大期望</span>，应该没那么好。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They've <span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">got Mr Mason's hopes up</span>, let him think he had a future.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他们<span style="color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">给了梅森先生希望</span>，让他以为又有了光明的未来。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">10.Forget I mentioned it.</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我没说吧；当我没提过；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: 87);box-sizing: border-box;">Forget I mentioned it. </span>It is not my place. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-What?</p><p style="white-space: 87);box-sizing: border-box;">当我没提过。</span>这与我无关。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;max-width: 100%;"></section></section></section></sectio</section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Molecule</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈmɒlɪkjuːl $ ˈmɑː-/  n. 分子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">辨析：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">molecule: 指物质中保持原物质的一切化学性质，能独立存在的最小微粒，即分子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">atom: 指元素的最小粒子，其体积比molecule小。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">particle: 指任何物质的微粒，引申指任何小的部分。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">speck: 一般指“微点”或“微粒”，可引申指“斑点、污点”。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">grain: 通常指能为肉眼清楚看到的颗粒，比上述几个词所表“粒”的体积大。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">chlorophyll  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'klɔːrəfɪl/   n.叶绿素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Show up 显露出来；出现，露面（= appear）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：At this point, they show up to my office.  这时候，他们跑来我的办公室。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be good at ≈ do well in    擅长        be bad at 不擅长</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">soak up </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.吸收，吸干〔液体〕</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：He used a towel to soak up the blood.他用毛巾把血吸掉。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.晒太阳，沐日光浴</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.全身心融入，感受:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Go to a sidewalk cafe, order coffee, and soak up the atmosphere .</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">找一家街头咖啡馆，点上一杯咖啡，让自己融入周围的环境。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.〔迅速而又轻松地〕吸收，学会:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Children soak up language incredibly quickly.小孩子学语言快得让人难以置信。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the more… , the more..    越…，就越…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：The more they learn, the more they want to learn。他们越学习，就越想学习。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the+比较级，the+比较级   也表示：越…，越…</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：The harder you work, the greater progress you will make. 你越用功，进步就越大。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">wavelength  n.〔无线电的、声波、光波等的〕波长</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">be on the same /be on a different wavelength  （informal）〔与其他人的观点、感情〕相投/不合:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Dad is just on a different wavelength from me. 爸爸和我就是没有共同语言。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Be composed of  由…构成；由…组成的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：The legal system is composed of people, and people make mistakes.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">法律制度是由人组成的，而人是会犯错误的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Compose  v. 作（曲）; 写信/诗/讲稿等:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Compose a letter to your local paper stating your views on an issue of your choice.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">选一个题材给当地的报纸写信谈谈你的意见。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bounce </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ bauns /  v.（使）弹起，（使）反弹，（使）弹跳；(光，声音等)反射:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">bounce off  弹跳，反射</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：The radio signals are bounced off a satellite. 无线电信号从卫星上反射回来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bounce  n.弹性，弹力; 活力，精力，朝气:</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：The ball had completely lost its bounce. 这球已经完全失去了弹力。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举例：Exercise is great. I feel like there's a new bounce in my step.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">运动真好，我感觉到自己的脚步轻快有力起来。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(206, 169, 203);padding: 10px;box-shadow: rgb(204, 204, 204) 2.6px 2.6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Thursday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">You may have learned that leaves are green because they <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">are</em> fu</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">ll of a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> green molecule called</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"> <span style="background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">chlorophyll – it’s the reason for the greenne</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">ss o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">f plants, from moss-green moss to grass-green</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"> <span style="background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">grass to ever-green evergreen. And the reason chlorophyll is so incredibly popular–showing</span> <span style="background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">u</span></span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">p i</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">n nearly every plan</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">n Earth–is that it’s goo</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d a</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> soaking up sunlight.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">你可能知道叶子是绿色的是因为叶子中有一种绿色的分子叫做叶绿素</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">----</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">这就是植物为什么是绿色的原因，从绿色苔藓到绿色草类再到四季常青的植物。叶绿素非常受欢迎</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">---</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">在地球上几乎每一个植物上都表现出来了。原因是因为它善于吸收阳光。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">The more light a plant gets, the more energy it has to make sugar an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> grow tulips an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> kumquats</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"> <span style="background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">an</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> do all <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">the </em>other things plants do.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">吸收越多的阳光，植物就有越多的能量去制造糖类，长出郁金香，金桔以及所有其他植物能做的。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">But wai</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> secon</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">: doesn</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">’t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> the fact <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that</em> chlorophyll is green mean <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">that</em> it’s actually bad at absorbing green light? I mean, sunlight is compose</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">f </span></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">the whole rainbow of colors, each a separate wavelength, an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> the colors we see when we loo</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">k at a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> leaf are the wavelengths that leaf isn’t absorbing — that is, they are the ones that bounce off the leaf and reach our eyes.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">但是等一下：是不是因为叶绿素是绿色的，对于吸收绿光是不利的？我的意思是阳光包含了彩虹中的所有颜色，每一种颜色都有一个单独的波长，当我们看见一片叶子的颜色就是叶子不能吸收的波长。也就是，光波经过叶子的反射到达我们的视线的颜色。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">Chlorophyll is grea</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a</em></span></span><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> absorbing reds and blues, but if i</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">were really awesome, wouldn</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">’t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> i</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> absorb all colors of light, green included, giving u</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> world full of black moss an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> black grass an</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> ever black trees?</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">叶绿素善于吸收红光和蓝光，但是如果它真的很厉害，它会不会吸收所有的光线，包括绿光在内，让我们的世界都长满了黑苔藓，黑色草和常黑的树？</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">So why aren’t leaves black? And since they apparently don’t have to be black, what’s</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);box-sizing: border-box;"> <span style="background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">stopping them <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">from</em> being red or blue instead? Is green just Nature’s favor</span></span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">ite</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;"> color, or is there something special about those wavelengths of light? The short answer is that we don’t know for sure.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">为什么叶子不是黑色的？显然他们不会为黑色，什么阻止它们变成红色或者蓝色呢？难道绿色是大自然最喜爱的颜色，还是这些光波有什么特别之处？简短的回答是，我们不确定是什么。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But what she noticed first was a bright red wooden tray with a number of rings on it. They were in pairs - a yellow one and a green one together, then a little space, and then another yellow one and another green one. They were no bigger than ordinary rings, and no one could help noticing them because they were so bright. They were the most beautiful shiny little things you can imagine. If Polly had been a very little younger she would have wanted to put one in her mouth.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">然而，她首先注意到的是一只红得发亮的木托盘，里面有几只戒指。这些戒指成对放着，一枚黄的和一枚绿的挨在一起隔了一点距离，又是一枚黄的和一枚绿的挨在一起。它们只不过像普通戒指那么大，但由于太亮了，谁也不会看不见。这些小戒指闪着你能想像的最共丽的光彩。如果波莉再小一点儿，她说不定会草一枚放进嘴里。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">贝斯：今天早晨我听到老板为了什么原因在跟迈克发脾气。你知道怎么回事吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">萨利：史蒂夫说迈克做错了事又试图掩盖它，被老板发现了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">贝斯：为什么他不坦白说出来？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">萨利：我想他害怕被辞退。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">贝斯：可是做错事的时候最重要的是说出来这样问题才能得到解决。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">萨利：我确信迈克一定希望你早一些跟他说这些话。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">贝斯：他不会再做错了，迈克不是傻瓜，只有傻瓜才会重复同样的错误。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">萨利：你总是那么聪明，能提出一些好建议。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">贝斯：但是要记住，就算最聪明的人也有犯错的时候。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beth: I heard the boss yelling at Mike for some reason earlier today. Do you know what it was about?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sally: Steve says that Mike made a mistake and then tried to cover it, but the boss found out.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beth: Why didn't he just own up and tell someone?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sally: He was too scared that he would be fired, I suppose.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beth: But when you have made a mistake, it is important to tell someone so that it can be fixed.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sally: I bet that Mike wished you had told him that earlier.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beth: He won't do that again - Mike is not a fool, and only fools make the same mistake twice.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sally: As always you are the smart one with the good advice.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Beth: But remember, even the smartest person makes mistakes sometimes!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Just between you and me, she wears too much make-up.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">________________，我觉得她的妆太浓了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">别告诉别人哦</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: -apple-system, 低调点！</strong></section><section><br/></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;font-style: normal;text-align: justify;font-size: 16px;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-weight: PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> /ˌkiːp ʌp əˈpɪərənsə̇z/</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to pretend that everything in your life is still as happy and successful as it used to be, even though you have suffered some kind of trouble or loss:</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">简单点儿就是：<em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to pretend something is true</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">来看几个句子~</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He tries to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong>, but he lives entirely off borrowed money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他强装<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表面光鲜亮丽</strong>，其实他一直在靠着借钱生活。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know we are just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keeping up appearances</strong>, but I just wanted to give you a chance to fall in love with me first.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道我们仅仅是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">装装样子</strong>，我只是希望你能先爱上我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway, we'd better <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong> before Miss Li leaves.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">无论如何，在李老师走之前，我们最好<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做做样子</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看了例句，大家现在知道“做样子，做好表面功夫”用英语如何表达了吧～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section rgb(102, 102, 102);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展</strong></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel /ʌnˈrævl/</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel(sth)</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">if you unravel threads that are twisted, woven or knitted, or if they unravel, they become separated （把缠或织在一起的线）解开，拆散，松开</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> unraveled</strong> the string and wound it into a ball. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她把绳子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">解开，</strong>绕成了一个球。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">(of a system, plan, relationship, etc. 系统、计划、关系等 ) to start to fail or no longer stay together as a whole 解体；崩溃；瓦解</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He never noticed that their relationship was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unraveling</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他从未想过他们的关系会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">崩塌</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to explain sth that is difficult to understand or is mysterious; to become clearer or easier to understand 阐释；说明；澄清；变得清楚易懂</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The discovery will help scientists <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel</strong> the mystery of the Ice Age. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这一发现将有助于科学家<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">揭开</strong>冰川时代的奥秘。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">(满眼不安)的样子</strong></span></section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>He’s got the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">look of</strong> a film star now, but he was a real ugly duckling as a child.他现在一副电影明星<strong style="box-sizing: has not been completely finished or explained </em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">（故事等的）悬念，未了结的部份，未交代清楚的情节</em></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align:
