style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Like my friend Bree Van De Kamp. I remember the easy confidence of her smile, the gentle elegance of her hands, the refined warmth of her voice. But what I remember most about Bree. . . Rex, wasn't that lovely? . . . was the look of fear in her eyes. Bree had started to realize her world was unraveling, and for a woman who despised loose ends, that was unacceptable. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Rex. Rex. You need to get up. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's not even light out. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please hurry. If the kids see you sleeping down here, they're going to start asking questions. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Let 'em ask. I don't care anymore. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, I care. They don't need to be burdened with our marital problems while we're working things out, the least we can do is try to <span style="color: rgb(255, 202, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong></span>. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, yeah. Appearances. I keep forgetting about appearances. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, Rex, you look so tired. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I didn't sleep. This damn thing is so uncomfortable. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, why don't you move back upstairs and sleep in our bed? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We're in marriage counseling, Bree. I think that would confuse things. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's just, I miss you. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know you do. Of course, if I don't start getting some sleep pretty soon I'll be forced to move back upstairs out of sheer exhaustion. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Yes, Bree was afraid of many things, but if there was one thing she wasn't afraid of, it was a challenge.</p></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" -3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 4px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(248, 200, 37);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 0%;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;padding: 0px 13px;color: rgb(102, 102, 102);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> /ˌkiːp ʌp əˈpɪərənsə̇z/</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to pretend that everything in your life is still as happy and successful as it used to be, even though you have suffered some kind of trouble or loss:</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">简单点儿就是：<em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to pretend something is true</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">来看几个句子~</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgb(71, 193, 168);box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He tries to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong>, but he lives entirely off borrowed money.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他强装<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">表面光鲜亮丽</strong>，其实他一直在靠着借钱生活。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I know we are just <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keeping up appearances</strong>, but I just wanted to give you a chance to fall in love with me first.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我知道我们仅仅是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">装装样子</strong>，我只是希望你能先爱上我。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Anyway, we'd better <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">keep up appearances</strong> before Miss Li leaves.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">无论如何，在李老师走之前，我们最好<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">做做样子</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看了例句，大家现在知道“做样子，做好表面功夫”用英语如何表达了吧～</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.75" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdtn0xkTqhjPMb8YBzUJhQ38aMmu5tmTiaSsHheLojJGIXKh5X4URL3EOoQDfC0Puib8kKUVeEH0uhA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>同名影视剧，大家可以看一看～<section style="box-sizing: border-box;">接下来我们来拓展其他有用的表达～</section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: left;justify-content: flex-start;margin: 10px 0%;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 33px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;align-self: center;line-height: 0;background-color: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: rotateZ(37deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(37deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(37deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(37deg);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="justify-content: flex-start;transform: translate3d(8px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(8px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(8px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(8px, 0px, 0px);margin: 2px 0% -3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 4px;height: 22px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(248, 200, 37);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 16px;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(74, 187, 168) 9px -6px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: auto;align-self: center;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;justify-content: flex-start;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;padding: 0px 13px;color: rgb(102, 102, 102);letter-spacing: 1px;line-height: 1;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展</strong></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel /ʌnˈrævl/</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel(sth)</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">if you unravel threads that are twisted, woven or knitted, or if they unravel, they become separated （把缠或织在一起的线）解开，拆散，松开</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"> unraveled</strong> the string and wound it into a ball. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她把绳子<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">解开，</strong>绕成了一个球。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">(of a system, plan, relationship, etc. 系统、计划、关系等 ) to start to fail or no longer stay together as a whole 解体；崩溃；瓦解</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He never noticed that their relationship was <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unraveling</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他从未想过他们的关系会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">崩塌</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3- <em style="box-sizing: border-box;">to explain sth that is difficult to understand or is mysterious; to become clearer or easier to understand 阐释；说明；澄清；变得清楚易懂</em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The discovery will help scientists <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">unravel</strong> the mystery of the Ice Age. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这一发现将有助于科学家<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">揭开</strong>冰川时代的奥秘。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">what I remember most about XX is</strong></span></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关于XX记忆犹新的是</strong></span></section><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">What I remember most about</strong> our marriage <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">is</strong> that you said your love would last forever.</p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关于</strong>我们的婚姻，<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">最难忘的一件事</strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">就是</strong>你说过会爱我到永远。</section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">the look of (fear in her eyes) ... </strong></span></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">(满眼不安)的样子</strong></span></section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>He’s got the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">look of</strong> a film star now, but he was a real ugly duckling as a child.他现在一副电影明星<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">的模样</strong>，小时候他可真是只丑小鸭。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">By the looks of it</strong>, it hasn't been moved in some time.<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">这样子看起来</strong>有一段时间没动过了。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">loose end</strong></span></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">未了结的部份</strong></span></section><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">a part of sth such as a story that has not been completely finished or explained </em><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">（故事等的）悬念，未了结的部份，未交代清楚的情节</em></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.5622951" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKdtn0xkTqhjPMb8YBzUJhQ3oMeFynziaJHLjrPNF0iaWf9D9icCoXFhfnH2nDfzk54QZK4vUYTotq3Kw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="610" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>The play has too many <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">loose ends</strong>. 这部剧有太多<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">地方未交代清楚</strong>。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/>There are still <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a few loose ends</strong> to tie up (= a few things to finish). 还有<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">几件小事</strong>需要了结。<br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">It's not even light out.</strong></span></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">天还没亮呢。</strong></span></section><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be burdened with </strong></span></section><section style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(71, 193, 168);text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">承受</strong></span></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.6153846" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKdtn0xkTqhjPMb8YBzUJhQ3u8evsWp0l86viaA6PdPV4UGlNwaWFS149unRkRNj6MCS6Yct6icYXfOw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="650" 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary &amp; Phrase</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Speculate</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'spekjʊleɪt/ US/'spɛkjə'let/ (vt.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">If you speculate about something, you make guesses about its nature or identity, or about what might happen. 猜测</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Some speculated that Putin was undergoing cosmetic surgery.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">许多人猜测普京正在接受整容手术。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Serendipity</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ˌser(ə)n'dɪpɪtɪ/ US/ˌsɛrən'dɪpəti/(n.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">~ is the luck some people have in finding or creating interesting or valuable things by chance. 运气; 走运 [文学性]</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：What an amazing story of serendipity!</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">真是无心插柳柳成荫呀！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Tips:Serendipity means a "happy accident" or "pleasant surprise":</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Archae</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'ɑ:kiəu/ (prefix)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">ancient, primitive</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子： </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">archaeology （n.）考古学</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Archaic（adj.）古代的；古风的；古体的  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">single-celled  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A unicellular organism, also known as a single-celled organism单细胞</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">minus-green </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK US /'maɪnəs/ '</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">without: lacking in or deprived of something欠缺的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：He came minus his tools, so he couldn't do much work.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他没有带工具，所以干不了什么活</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Bacteria(bacterium)　</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/bæk'tɪərɪə/ US/bæk'tɪrɪə/(n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">very small organisms. Some bacteria can cause disease. 细菌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Bacteria is something invisible to the eye.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">细菌是肉眼看不见的东西。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Molecule </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'mɒlɪkju:l/ US/'mɑlɪkjul/ (n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A molecule is the smallest amount of a chemical substance which can exist by itself. 分子</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：A molecule is made up of atoms.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">分子由原子组成。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Chlorophyll </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'klɔːrəfɪl/ US/'klɔrəfɪl/ （n.）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">any of a group of green pigments found in photosynthetic organisms; there are four naturally occurring forms 叶绿素</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Chlorophyll helps trees make sugar from sunlight.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有了阳光，叶绿素就能帮助树木制造糖分。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Biochemical </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(adj.)UK/'baɪo'kɛmɪkl/ US/'baɪo'kɛmɪkl/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">of or relating to biochemistry; involving chemical processes in living organisms生物化学的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Starvation brings biochemical changes in the body.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">饥饿引起体内的生化变化</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Rivalry </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'raɪv(ə)lrɪ/ US/'raɪvlri/(n.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the act of competing as for profit or a prize竞争; 斗争</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Now, rivalry has to be replaced by social capital.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如今社会资本已经代替了竞争。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">emerge from </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/ɪ'mɜːdʒ/ US/ɪ'mɝdʒ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">自…出现；从…显露出来</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：The sun soon emerged from behind the clouds.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">太阳不久从云朵后钻出。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Mighty </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UK/'maɪtɪ/ US/'maɪti/ (adj.)</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">strong and powerful: of great strength and poweradj. 有力的；有势力的；强有力的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Is the truth mighty, and will it prevail?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个真理强大吗？它终会取胜吗？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">flawless </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈflɔ:lɪs/ /'flɔləs/(adj.) </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">perfect: without any blemish or imperfection  完美的；无瑕疵的；无裂缝的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Flow -less</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：Either we have a complete flawless record, or it's useless.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如果你不是完美无瑕，那你就是一无是处。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">get by </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">just manage to keep going: to manage to survive or just make ends meet过得去；过活</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">举个例子：But you can get by on one kidney, right?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">但是 一个肾脏仍然能够继续撑下去 对吗?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: other biochemical advantages over the purple competition.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(96, 96, 96);background: white;box-sizing: border-box;">从长远来看，据我们所知，叶绿素不吸收绿光是浪费的，也可能是它胜过紫色竞争者的生化优势。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span emerg</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);background: white;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Digory looked and saw a faded photograph: it showed the face of an old woman in a bonnet. And he could now remember that he had once seen a photo of the same face in an old drawer, at home, in the country. He had asked his Mother who it was and Mother had not seemed to want to talk about the subject much. It was not at all a nice face, Digory thought, though of course with those early photographs one could never really tell.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迪格雷望过去，着见一幅褪色的头像：一位头戴无边有带女式帽的老太太。他想起，在乡下家中的一个旧抽屉里也见过她的一张头像。他曾经问过妈妈她是谁，但妈妈好像不大愿意谈这个话题。迪格雷想，虽然不能单凭那些旧照片来分辨美丑：但那张脸的确一点儿也不好看。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迈克尔：先生，见到你真的很高兴。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比利：是么？我能为您做点什么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迈克尔：你可以去为客人选择合适的食物让食品配送公司去准备。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比利：我们今年有自助餐么？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迈克尔：是的，先生，您可以根据自己的胃口选择，但您要决定餐桌该上哪些食品。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比利：选择太多了。我能不能让别人来做这事儿呢？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">迈克尔：对不起，先生，不可以。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">比利：高处不胜寒啊。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Michael: Sir, I sure am glad to see you.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Billy: Really? How may I be of service to you?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Michael: You should select the appropriate food for craft services to prepare for the guests.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Billy: Are we having a buffet this year?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Michael: Yes sir, it is serving yourself, but you still need to decide what food to put on the banquet tables.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Billy: So many choices. Can't I give the responsibility to someone else?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Michael: No, sorry, you can't.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Billy: It is lonely at the top.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's not ___________to tell me how to do my job.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">用不着你来告诉我怎样做我自己的工作。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding:
